    这是一个非常流行的模型。它广泛应用于Kaggle和Netflix Prize等竞赛中 。事实上，它非常有效，以至于即使是现代专注于表格数据的深度学习论文，也被要求将结果与XGBoost进行比较 。它仍然是结构化数据问题的最先进基准。这是一个你应该掌握的强大工具。
## Week 5 Lecture 4
  - [20:19 - 20:20] **Introduction to Tree Construction and Residuals**

    Presently, we focus on the performance based on the residuals. Remember, we built a first model, and then we build a second one. The combination of the first and second models acts as our new prediction. So, based on this additive prediction approach, today's lecture will show you exactly how to build these trees. You will see that we use a specific method. Here we choose the tree structure. The idea is the same as we discussed before, but there are some differences in the details. So now, let's see how to build the tree in each stage. We also have some controls on the size of the tree.

    目前，我们关注基于残差（residuals）的性能。记得吗，我们建立了第一个模型，然后建立第二个模型。第一个和第二个模型的组合就成为了我们要的新预测结果。所以，基于这种加法预测的方法，今天的课程将向你们展示究竟如何构建这些树。你们会看到我们使用了一种特定的方法。在这里我们选择树结构。这背后的核心理念和我们之前讨论的是一样的，但在细节上有一些不同。现在，让我们来看看如何在每个阶段构建树。我们对树的大小也有一些控制机制。

  - [20:20 - 20:21] **Calculating the Node Score using Negative Residuals**

    When we build a tree, we start from the root and proceed node by node. I assume you know the basics of that process. Key symbols here involve the "negative residuals." We define `g_i` as `ŷ_i - y_i` (the predicted value minus the actual value). These are what we call the active or negative residuals because we are fitting the tree to them. We then calculate a "Node Score" from these residuals using a specific formula. For each example, we have a residual. We sum them all together, square that sum, and then divide by the number of samples plus Lambda (`λ`). Lambda here is a hyperparameter.

    当我们构建一棵树时，我们从根节点开始，逐个节点地进行。我假设你们已经了解了这个过程的基础知识。这里的关键符号涉及“负残差”（negative residuals）。我们将 `g_i` 定义为 `ŷ_i - y_i`（预测值减去实际值）。这些被称为负残差，因为我们要用树来拟合它们。然后，我们使用特定的公式根据这些残差计算“节点分数”（Node Score）。对于每个样本，我们都有一个残差。我们将它们全部加在一起，对总和进行平方，然后除以样本数量加上 Lambda (`λ`)。这里的 Lambda 是一个超参数。

  - [20:21 - 20:23] **Strategy for Splitting Nodes**

    We will see how to obtain the values of this hyperparameter later. Now, you see, in the original dataset, we have many features. Here, we want to test every possible feature to find the best partition or split in the node. Remember, we build the tree from the root, then we split and split again. For example, when we reach a specific node, we calculate the score. Then we need to find out what is the best partition—the left and right partition. We have a number of features available, so we have to try every possible feature. We try every possible partition split according to that feature because we don't know beforehand which one is best.

    我们将稍后讨论如何获取这个超参数的值。现在，你们看，在原始数据集中，我们有很多特征。在这里，我们要测试每一个可能的特征，以找到节点中最好的划分或分裂点。记得吗，我们从根节点开始建树，然后不断地分裂。例如，当我们到达一个特定的节点时，我们计算分数。然后我们需要找出什么是最好的划分——即左边和右边的划分。我们要利用所有可用的特征，所以我们必须尝试每一个可能的特征。我们尝试根据该特征进行的每一个可能的划分，因为我们事先不知道哪一个是最好的。

  - [20:23 - 20:25] **Numeric Example: Splitting on Feature X**

    Now, let's consider one dimension, one feature; we call it `J`. There is a value we use to split the data into two parts. Say, for example, looking at the data on the slide, if we use a value of 6 as a cutoff, then we split these samples into two parts. The first part, let's call it `A`, contains all the samples with a value greater than or equal to 6. In this feature `X`, we have already sorted the samples according to their values. So, "greater than or equal to 6" means it contains these two specific samples (where X is 7 and 9). If we use 6 as a cutoff, these samples go here. Then we calculate the score for this new node `A` in the same manner. But when we calculate this score, we just use the residuals for the samples in `A`.

    现在，让我们考虑一个维度，一个特征；我们称之为 `J`。我们使用一个值将数据分成两部分。比如，看幻灯片上的数据，如果我们使用 6 作为截断值（cutoff），那么我们将这些样本分成两部分。第一部分，我们称之为 `A`，包含所有值大于或等于 6 的样本。在这个特征 `X` 中，我们已经根据它们的值对样本进行了排序。所以，“大于或等于 6”意味着它包含这两个特定的样本（X 为 7 和 9 的样本）。如果我们使用 6 作为截断值，这些样本就归到这里。然后我们以同样的方式计算这个新节点 `A` 的分数。但是当我们计算这个分数时，我们只使用 `A` 中样本的残差。

  - [20:25 - 20:26] **Calculating Gain with Lambda (`λ`) and Gamma (`γ`)**

    When we calculate the score for the other part, `B` (samples where X < 6), we just use the residuals in `B`. So, for the score formula, the numerator is the square of the sum of residuals in that group. The denominator is the number of samples in that group (for example, 2 for group `A`) plus Lambda. This Lambda is the same hyperparameter used everywhere. Then we consider the "Gain" of the split. The Gain is calculated as the sum of the scores in the two parts (Score A + Score B), minus the score of the parent node (Score before split), and then minus another parameter, Gamma (`γ`). Gamma is another hyperparameter.

    当我们计算另一部分 `B`（X < 6 的样本）的分数时，我们只使用 `B` 中的残差。所以，对于分数公式，分子是该组残差之和的平方。分母是该组中的样本数量（例如组 `A` 是 2）加上 Lambda。这个 Lambda 是到处使用的同一个超参数。然后我们考虑这次分裂的“增益”（Gain）。增益的计算方法是两部分的分数之和（分数 A + 分数 B），减去父节点的分数（分裂前的分数），然后再减去另一个参数，Gamma (`γ`)。Gamma 是另一个超参数。

  - [20:26 - 20:28] **Decision Rule: To Split or Not to Split**

    We consider every possible feature and every possible cutoff, and then we choose the best one. We want the one that gives the largest Gain. This corresponds to the best partition of the samples. If this Gain is positive, then we perform the split. If the Gain is not positive (negative), then we just stop there. We treat this node as a leaf node. The value for this leaf node is calculated this way: the sum of residuals divided by the number of samples `K` plus Lambda `λ`, and there is a negative sign in front. This is how we determine whether to split in each node or establish a leaf value.

    我们考虑每一个可能的特征和每一个可能的截断值，然后我们选择最好的一个。我们想要那个能产生最大增益（Gain）的划分。这对应于样本的最佳划分。如果这个增益是正的，那么我们就进行分裂。如果增益不是正的（是负的），那么我们就在那里停止。我们将这个节点视为叶节点。叶节点的值是这样计算的：残差之和除以样本数量 `K` 加上 Lambda `λ`，并且前面有一个负号。这就是我们如何决定在每个节点是否分裂或确立叶子值的方法。

  - [20:28 - 20:30] **Walkthrough of the Numeric Example (Slide 51)**

    Let's look at this example with 5 samples. We focus on this feature `X`. These are the true values `y` and the current predicted values `ŷ`. The negative residual is equal to the predicted value minus the true value (`ŷ - y`). So, for the first example, it is -0.5 (2.5 - 3). For the second one, it is 0.5 (2.5 - 2). For the third one, it is -3.5 (2.5 - 6). Is this clear how to calculate this negative residual? Now, we will calculate the score for this parent node. You will see we just sum all the negative residuals. This one corresponds to this, this one to that... we square the sum. There are 5 samples. Lambda is a hyperparameter, and for investigation purposes here, we set Lambda to be 1. So therefore, we get this number: the score is 30.375.

    让我们来看看这个有 5 个样本的例子。我们关注特征 `X`。这是真实值 `y` 和当前的预测值 `ŷ`。负残差等于预测值减去真实值（`ŷ - y`）。所以，对于第一个例子，它是 -0.5（2.5 - 3）。对于第二个，它是 0.5（2.5 - 2）。对于第三个，它是 -3.5（2.5 - 6）。如何计算这个负残差清楚了吗？现在，我们将计算这个父节点的分数。你们会看到我们只是将所有负残差相加。这个对应这个，那个对应那个……我们将总和平方。这里有 5 个样本。Lambda 是一个超参数，为了便于研究，这里我们将 Lambda 设为 1。因此，我们得到这个数字：分数是 30.375。

  - [20:30 - 20:32] **Identifying Possible Split Points**

    Is this clear? We focus on one feature, and we calculate the score for the whole dataset (or the samples contained in the node). In the very beginning, this node contains all samples. But after a split, a node will contain only some samples. This example focuses on these 5 samples, so this is the score. Now we consider the split. For this 5-sample dataset, how many possible splits are there? The samples are sorted according to the values of feature `X`: 2, 3, 5, 7, 9. So if we split between 2 and 3, we get one possible split. Then we have another possible split between 3 and 5. If we choose, say, 3.5, we get another one. And another one between 5 and 7, and another between 7 and 9. So that is four possible splits for this feature.

    这清楚吗？我们专注于一个特征，并计算整个数据集（或节点中包含的样本）的分数。最开始，这个节点包含所有样本。但在分裂之后，一个节点将只包含部分样本。这个例子关注这 5 个样本，这就是它的分数。现在我们考虑分裂。对于这 5 个样本的数据集，有多少种可能的分裂？样本是根据特征 `X` 的值排序的：2、3、5、7、9。所以如果我们在 2 和 3 之间分裂，我们得到一种可能的分裂。在 3 和 5 之间我们有另一种可能的分裂。如果我们选择，比如说 3.5，我们得到另一种。在 5 和 7 之间还有一种，在 7 和 9 之间也有一种。所以对于这个特征，有四种可能的分裂。

  - [20:32 - 20:35] **Calculating Scores for the Left and Right Children**

    Now, we just use 6 as a cutoff for this example. I use this one to explain. So `A` is the set of samples with `X` greater than or equal to 6. This refers to the last two samples (7 and 9). `B` is the samples with `X` less than 6, which are the first three samples. This split is clear: we use 6 as a cutoff value. Then we calculate the score for part `A`. Part `A` contains the last two samples. The residuals are -5.5 and -4.5. So the sum is -10. -10 squared is 100, right? The Lambda now is 1. The number of samples is 2. So the denominator is 2 + 1 = 3. The result is 100 divided by 3, which is 33.33. Similarly, `B` contains the first three samples, so we use these three residuals: -0.5, 0.5, and -3.5. We sum them, square them, and divide by 3 (samples) plus Lambda (1). The value is 3.06.

    现在，在这个例子中我们只使用 6 作为截断值。我用这个来解释。所以 `A` 是 `X` 大于或等于 6 的样本集合。这指的是最后两个样本（7 和 9）。`B` 是 `X` 小于 6 的样本，也就是前三个样本。这个分裂很清楚：我们使用 6 作为截断值。然后我们计算 `A` 部分的分数。`A` 部分包含最后两个样本。残差是 -5.5 和 -4.5。所以总和是 -10。-10 的平方是 100，对吧？Lambda 现在是 1。样本数量是 2。所以分母是 2 + 1 = 3。结果是 100 除以 3，即 33.33。同样地，`B` 包含前三个样本，所以我们使用这三个残差：-0.5、0.5 和 -3.5。我们将它们相加，平方，然后除以 3（样本数）加上 Lambda（1）。这个值是 3.06。

  - [20:35 - 20:37] **Gain Calculation and Split Decision**

    Therefore, the Gain for this partition is 0.5 multiplied by (33.33 + 3.06 minus the parent score 30.375), and then minus Gamma (`γ`). Gamma is another hyperparameter, and we decided to set this to 0. Since the result is positive, it means it is a good split. If the Gain is negative, then we should stop. This is the condition to determine whether to split or not split based on the Gain value. A positive Gain implies a split. We want to increase the Gain, so positive means good. It implies we should split.

    因此，这个划分的增益（Gain）是 0.5 乘以（33.33 + 3.06 减去父节点分数 30.375），然后再减去 Gamma (`γ`)。Gamma 是另一个超参数，我们决定将其设为 0。因为结果是正的，这意味着这是一个好的分裂。如果增益是负的，那么我们就应该停止。这是根据增益值决定是否分裂的条件。正的增益意味着分裂。我们想要增加增益，所以正值意味着好。它意味着我们应该进行分裂。

  - [20:37 - 20:39] **Theoretical Basis and Leaf Values**

    In fact, this condition is controlled by this hyperparameter. There is some theory behind this formula. Basically, it controls the balance. If we stop splitting, we need to output a value in the node. We want to get this model such that it minimizes the error. If the tree gives a wrong prediction error, we want to fix it. We build many trees. Lambda controls the size or the complexity. Is the formula clear? We have these residuals, and this is how we compute this.

    事实上，这个条件是由这个超参数控制的。这个公式背后有一些理论依据。基本上，它控制着平衡。如果我们停止分裂，我们需要在节点中输出一个值。我们希望得到的模型能最小化误差。如果树给出了错误的预测误差，我们希望修正它。我们要建立很多棵树。Lambda 控制大小或复杂度。公式清楚了吗？我们有这些残差，这就是我们计算它的方式。

  - [20:39 - 20:42] **Calculating Leaf Output Values (Weights)**

    So now you see after this, we split the five samples into two nodes. One node has 2 samples (where X >= 6). The other has 3 samples (where X < 6). These two nodes, if we don't need to split them more, become leaves. Therefore, we need to calculate the optimal output value (prediction value) for each node. The calculation is also very straightforward. For node `B` (the left part), it has 3 samples. We just take the sum of residuals for samples in `B`: -0.5 + 0.5 + -3.5. Then we divide by the number of samples (3) plus Lambda (1), and apply a negative sign. This gives you the leaf value. That's why the leaf value is 7/8 (or 0.875). For the other node with 2 samples, we calculate the sum of residuals (-4.5 - 5.5 = -10), divide by (2+1), and apply the negative sign. So the value is 10/3.

    现在你们看到，在这之后，我们将五个样本分成了两个节点。一个节点有 2 个样本（X >= 6）。另一个有 3 个样本（X < 6）。这两个节点，如果我们不需要进一步分裂，就成为叶子节点。因此，我们需要计算每个节点的最佳输出值（预测值）。计算也非常简单。对于节点 `B`（左边部分），它有 3 个样本。我们只需取 `B` 中样本残差的总和：-0.5 + 0.5 + -3.5。然后我们除以样本数（3）加上 Lambda（1），并加上一个负号。这给出了叶子值。这就是为什么叶子值是 7/8（或 0.875）。对于另一个有 2 个样本的节点，我们计算残差之和（-4.5 - 5.5 = -10），除以（2+1），并加上负号。所以值是 10/3。

  - [20:42 - 20:44] **Scaling to Multiple Features and Full Trees**

    Is this video decision tree process clear? Here we just considered one feature, but if you have one million dimensions or many features, you just do this for every feature. You choose the best split from all possible splits across all features. You consider all possible splits and choose the best one. We want large Gains. When we choose the largest Gain, we then determine whether to split or not based on whether it's positive (after subtracting Gamma).

    这个视频决策树的过程清楚了吗？这里我们只考虑了一个特征，但如果你有一百万个维度或很多特征，你就对每个特征都这样做。你从所有特征的所有可能分裂中选择最好的一个。你考虑所有可能的分裂并选择最好的。我们想要大的增益。当我们选择了最大增益后，我们根据它是否为正（减去 Gamma 后）来决定是否分裂。

  - [20:44 - 20:46] **Hyperparameters: Trees, Learning Rate, Lambda, Gamma**

    There are key hyperparameters for building a tree. The first one, and most important, is how many trees you want. This one we cannot treat automatically; we have to assign it. We have to try different numbers. Also, there is a learning rate in front of each tree. The default is 0.3, but you also need to find the best weight for performance. Lambda is for regularization; a larger Lambda means stronger regularization, which means a simpler model. The purpose is to avoid overfitting. Gamma is another hyperparameter; a large Gamma implies fewer splits because if Gamma is big, the Gain needs to be more positive to split. This builds a shallower tree.

    构建树有一些关键的超参数。第一个，也是最重要的，是你想要多少棵树。这个我们无法自动处理；我们必须指定它。我们必须尝试不同的数量。此外，每棵树前面都有一个学习率（learning rate）。默认值是 0.3，但你也需要找到性能最佳的权重。Lambda 用于正则化；较大的 Lambda 意味着更强的正则化，也就意味着更简单的模型。目的是为了避免过拟合。Gamma 是另一个超参数；较大的 Gamma 意味着更少的分裂，因为如果 Gamma 很大，增益需要非常正才能进行分裂。这会构建出一棵较浅的树。

  - [20:46 - 20:51] **Hyperparameter Tuning Methods**

    How do we determine these? There is no cheap method for this. The straightforward method is to search over all possible parameter values. For example, for the learning rate, can you try these five possibilities: 0.1, 0.3, 0.6, 1.0? For the max depth (longest path from root to leaf), you can try 1, 3, 6, 10. This is the standard method for building XGBoost models—what we call Grid Search or Randomized Search. The principle is to build many trees and put them together.

    我们如何确定这些参数呢？这没有捷径。直接的方法是搜索所有可能的参数值。例如，对于学习率，你可以尝试这五种可能：0.1、0.3、0.6、1.0？对于最大深度（从根到叶的最长路径），你可以尝试 1、3、6、10。这是构建 XGBoost 模型的标准方法——我们称之为网格搜索（Grid Search）或随机搜索。其原则是构建许多树并将它们组合在一起。

  - [20:51 - 20:53] **XGBoost for Classification: Introduction**

    The only different thing now is when we use a different objective, like classification. It can be very dangerous if misunderstood. So, in the very beginning, we might again pick a base value like 0.5. We build a tree with one node outputting 0.5. I will explain this. Then we build the first tree, the second one, and so forth. The procedure is the same, only the condition is different. Let's see this simple dataset with only four samples for binary classification. There are two classes. One class has label 1, and the other class has label 0.

    现在唯一不同的是当我们使用不同的目标时，比如分类。如果理解错了可能会很危险。所以，在一开始，我们可能再次选择一个基准值，比如 0.5。我们建立一棵只有一个节点输出 0.5 的树。我会解释这一点。然后我们建立第一棵树，第二棵树，依此类推。过程是一样的，只是条件不同。让我们看看这个只有四个样本的简单数据集，用于二分类。有两个类别。一个类别的标签是 1，另一个类别的标签是 0。

  - [20:53 - 20:55] **Interpreting Labels as Probabilities**

    We can consider the dataset as providing probabilities. For example, being in Class 1 means the probability is 1. So Label 1 is a sample in Class 1 with probability 1. Label 0 is a sample with probability 0 for Class 1. Therefore, we interpret these labels as probability values. Basically, we train an XGBoost classifier to predict the probability that a sample belongs to Class 1. Everyone reports probabilities. For a sample in the first class, the model output probability should be very close to 1. For the other class, the model output probability is small, close to 0. If we can do this, the model is good. Is that clear? We don't really want to output just 0 or 1; that is hard. The model gives you a confidence.

    我们可以将数据集视为提供概率。例如，属于类别 1 意味着概率为 1。所以标签 1 是一个概率为 1 的类别 1 的样本。标签 0 是一个类别 1 概率为 0 的样本。因此，我们将这些标签解释为概率值。基本上，我们训练一个 XGBoost 分类器来预测样本属于类别 1 的概率。每个人都报告概率。对于第一类中的样本，模型输出的概率应该非常接近 1。对于另一类，模型输出的概率很小，接近 0。如果我们能做到这一点，模型就是好的。清楚了吗？我们并不真的想只输出 0 或 1；那太硬了。模型给你的是一个置信度。

  - [20:55 - 20:57] **Initial Prediction and Classification Residuals**

    In the very beginning, we choose 0.5 because, looking here, there are two samples in each class. The average value is 0.5. It's reasonable. If there is a large number of samples in Class 1, we might choose a different value, but 0.5 is a very reasonable average value. This is the prediction probability from the first base model. Then, to build the second tree, we use the negative residual. The negative residual is `p - y` (prediction minus label). Wait, actually, typically it is `y - p`, but let's look at the negative residual values. For the first sample (Class 1), it gives -0.5. For another, -0.5. For the third one in the other class (Class 0), the negative residual is 0.5. Then we can build the second tree using these values. This is similar to the regression tree, just playing with these small numbers.

    在一开始，我们选择 0.5，因为看这里，每个类别有两个样本。平均值是 0.5。这是合理的。如果类别 1 中有大量样本，我们可能会选择不同的值，但 0.5 是一个非常合理的平均值。这是第一个基础模型的预测概率。然后，为了构建第二棵树，我们使用负残差。负残差是 `p - y`（预测值减去标签）。对于第一个样本（类别 1），它给出 -0.5。对于另一个，也是 -0.5。对于另一类（类别 0）的第三个样本，负残差是 0.5。然后我们可以使用这些值来构建第二棵树。这与回归树类似，只是在处理这些小数字。

  - [20:58 - 21:01] **Calculating Node Scores for Classification (Gradient and Hessian)**

    Now, how do we calculate the score for this classification problem? The formula is slightly different. The top part (numerator) is the sum of residuals squared (`G^2`), which is the same as regression. But the bottom is very different. The bottom uses `H`. `H` is `p * (1 - p)`. Since our initial `p` is 0.5, `p * (1 - p)` is `0.5 * 0.5 = 0.25`. Since the first model is very simple and just outputs 0.5 for everyone, `H` is 0.25 for all terms. Thank you for pointing that out. So `G^2` is on top, and the bottom involves the sum of `H` plus Lambda. Lambda is set to 1 here.

    现在，我们要如何计算这个分类问题的分数呢？公式稍微有些不同。顶部部分（分子）是残差之和的平方（`G^2`），这与回归相同。但底部非常不同。底部使用的是 `H`。`H` 是 `p * (1 - p)`。因为我们要初始 `p` 是 0.5，`p * (1 - p)` 就是 `0.5 * 0.5 = 0.25`。因为第一个模型非常简单，对所有人只输出 0.5，所以所有项的 `H` 都是 0.25。谢谢你的指出。所以 `G^2` 在上面，底部涉及 `H` 之和加上 Lambda。这里 Lambda 设为 1。

  - [21:01 - 21:03] **Classification Split Example**

    Then we consider a split. There are 3 possible splits for this case. This samples are `X` smaller than 5. So 5 is here. Therefore, the first two samples go to one side, and the last two samples go to the other. This split is very natural because the top ones have small values for feature `X`, and the bottom ones have larger values. So we just cut at the bottom part. Then we calculate the score in the same way, just on a small scale. We calculate `G_A` (sum of residuals for A). For the first group, residuals are -0.5 and -0.5, so the sum is -1. `H_A` is sum of `p(1-p)`, so it is 0.25 + 0.25 = 0.5.

    然后我们考虑分裂。这种情况下有 3 种可能的分裂。这些样本的 `X` 小于 5。所以 5 在这里。因此，前两个样本去一边，后两个样本去另一边。这个分裂很自然，因为上面的样本特征 `X` 值较小，下面的值较大。所以我们就从下面切开。然后我们以同样的方式计算分数，只是规模变小了。我们计算 `G_A`（A 组的残差之和）。对于第一组，残差是 -0.5 和 -0.5，所以总和是 -1。`H_A` 是 `p(1-p)` 的总和，所以它是 0.25 + 0.25 = 0.5。

  - [21:03 - 21:06] **Score and Gain Calculation for Classification**

    So the score for part `A` is `(-1)^2` divided by `(0.5 + 1)`. The `+1` is Lambda. This gives `1 / 1.5` or `2/3`. For part `B`, the residuals are 0.5 and 0.5, sum is 1. `H` sum is also 0.5. So the score is also `1^2 / (0.5 + 1) = 2/3`. The Gain is the score of `A` plus score of `B` minus the score of the parent, divided by 2 (Note: the factor 1/2 appears in the Gain formula in the slide), minus Gamma (0). Since the result is positive, we perform some split. We consider all possible features and cutoffs, and find the best one.

    所以 `A` 部分的分数是 `(-1)^2` 除以 `(0.5 + 1)`。`+1` 是 Lambda。这得出 `1 / 1.5` 或 `2/3`。对于 `B` 部分，残差是 0.5 和 0.5，和是 1。`H` 的和也是 0.5。所以分数也是 `1^2 / (0.5 + 1) = 2/3`。增益是 `A` 的分数加上 `B` 的分数减去父节点的分数，除以 2（注：幻灯片中的增益公式里有 1/2 的系数），再减去 Gamma（0）。因为结果是正的，我们执行某种分裂。我们考虑所有可能的特征和截断值，并找到最好的一个。

  - [21:06 - 21:08] **Converting Leaf Weight to Probability (Sigmoid)**

    In this case, there are no further splits. So what is the output value? It means probability. How do we calculate the probability? We first calculate the leaf weight value `w` using the formula `w = -Sum(G) / (Sum(H) + Lambda)`. For the left leaf, this gives `2/3`. Then we compute the probability using the Sigmoid formula: `p = 1 / (1 + e^(-w))`. This gives `0.661`. Why do we use this complicated formula to get the probability? Because the theory works on the "log-odds" value. The optimization isn't directly on the probability `p`, but on the log-odds.

    在这种情况下，没有进一步的分裂。那么输出值是什么呢？它意味着概率。我们如何计算概率？我们首先使用公式 `w = -Sum(G) / (Sum(H) + Lambda)` 计算叶子权重值 `w`。对于左叶子，这得出 `2/3`。然后我们使用 Sigmoid 公式计算概率：`p = 1 / (1 + e^(-w))`。这得出 `0.661`。为什么我们要用这个复杂的公式来得到概率？因为理论是基于“对数几率”（log-odds）值的。优化不是直接针对概率 `p` 进行的，而是针对对数几率。

  - [21:08 - 21:12] **Log-Odds and Deep Learning Connection**

    If you take the log of `p / (1-p)`, that is the log-odds. The whole optimization theory works on this number, not directly on the probability. That's why we need to convert this log-odds value back to this probability. This is also a popular transformation function in deep learning and neural networks. We don't really work on the probability directly; we work on the log-odds because it is easier to work on mathematically. So if `log(p/(1-p)) = x`, then `p = 1 / (1 + e^(-x))`. This is the formula we use here. It converts the leaf score to probability.

    如果你取 `p / (1-p)` 的对数，那就是对数几率。整个优化理论是基于这个数字工作的，而不是直接基于概率。这就是为什么我们需要将这个对数几率值转换回概率。这也是深度学习和神经网络中一种流行的变换函数。我们并不真的直接处理概率；我们处理对数几率，因为这在数学上更容易处理。所以如果 `log(p/(1-p)) = x`，那么 `p = 1 / (1 + e^(-x))`。这就是我们在这里使用的公式。它将叶子分数转换为概率。

  - [21:12 - 21:16] **Conclusion and Advantages of XGBoost**

    So, building the tree for classification is the same as regression; you calculate gradients (residuals). The only difference is the leaf score formula involving `H` and the final conversion to probability using Sigmoid. In summary, XGBoost works well and can be used for very large datasets. It is based on good theory, has a regularization mechanism, and efficient split finding. It is also parallelizable, so you can work on large data using multiple processors. Although it has been around for 10 years, it is still a very good method for tabular data and competitive modeling. I think that's enough for today. Thank you.

    所以，构建分类树与回归树是一样的；你计算梯度（残差）。唯一的区别是涉及 `H` 的叶子分数公式以及最后使用 Sigmoid 转换为概率。总之，XGBoost 效果很好，可以用于非常大的数据集。它基于良好的理论，有正则化机制，以及高效的分裂查找。它也是可并行的，所以你可以使用多处理器处理大数据。虽然它已经出现了 10 年，但对于表格数据和竞技建模来说，它仍然是一个非常好的方法。我想今天就讲到这里。谢谢。
## Week 6 Lecture 5
  - [18:00:06 - 18:02:20] **Introduction to Machine Learning Paradigms**

    Okay. So, how was your holiday? Busy? Hmm. Okay. Let's start today's lecture. We have a new topic: Clustering. So, there are two main types of machine learning tasks: supervised learning and unsupervised learning. In a supervised learning task, a labeled training dataset is provided. We use this training dataset to learn a classifier, let's call it `f`, which can then be applied to a new sample for prediction. So far, the basic models we have learned—such as linear regression, K-Nearest Neighbors (KNN), and decision tree-based methods—are what we call traditional machine learning models. You might wonder whether these models are powerful enough. Actually, when you combine them with feature mapping, we can construct a much more complex model.

    好的。大家假期过得怎么样？很忙吗？嗯。好的。我们开始今天的课程。我们有一个新话题：聚类（Clustering）。机器学习任务主要有两种类型：监督学习（Supervised Learning）和无监督学习（Unsupervised Learning）。在监督学习任务中，我们有带标签的训练数据集。我们使用这个训练数据集来学习一个分类器 `f`，这个分类器随后可以应用于新的样本进行预测。到目前为止，我们学习的线性回归、K近邻（KNN）以及基于决策树的方法，都属于所谓的传统机器学习模型。你们可能会想，这些模型是否足够强大。实际上，当我们将它们与特征映射（Feature Mapping）结合时，我们可以构建出更复杂的模型。

  - [18:02:21 - 18:05:21] **Feature Mapping and Interaction Features**

    For example, to capture the interaction between two symptoms for disease prediction, we can introduce an interaction feature into the model. Let's look at this original training dataset. We can insert a new feature called "Interaction." This is obtained from the "Fever" symptoms and the "Sore-throat" symptoms. Basically, we just multiply these two features to get the interaction feature. So, `1 * 0` gives us `0`; `1 * 1` gives us `1`; `0 * 1` gives us `0`, and so on. In this way, we generate a new feature. Now, if we learn a model for this new dataset, it might look like a linear model, `f = w_0 + w_1*m + w_2*x + w_3*y + w_4*xy`. However, with respect to the original dataset, this is not a linear model; it is actually a polynomial model. Is that clear? Because there is a polynomial term in the function—`x` times `y` is a degree-two function. Therefore, by combining feature mapping with a simple linear model, we can get a complex model. This is why feature mapping is very important. Even if we just learn a linear model or a decision tree—which is essentially a piecewise linear model—we can handle complex relationships if we play with feature mapping properly.

    例如，为了捕捉两种症状之间的相互作用以进行疾病预测，我们可以在模型中引入一个交互特征。看看这个原始训练数据集，我们可以插入一个名为“交互（Interaction）”的新特征。这个特征是通过“发烧（Fever）”症状和“喉咙痛（Sore-throat）”症状获得的。基本上，我们将这两个特征相乘得到交互特征。比如，`1` 乘以 `0` 得到 `0`；`1` 乘以 `1` 得到 `1`；`0` 乘以 `1` 得到 `0`，依此类推。通过这种方式，我们得到了一个新的特征。现在，如果我们在这个新数据集上学习一个模型，它看起来像是一个线性模型 `f = w_0 + w_1*m + w_2*x + w_3*y + w_4*xy`。然而，相对于原始数据集来说，这不是一个线性模型，实际上它是一个多项式模型。清楚了吗？因为函数中有一个多项式项——`x` 乘以 `y` 是一个二次函数。因此，通过将特征映射与简单的线性模型结合，我们可以得到一个复杂的模型。这就是为什么特征映射非常重要。即使我们只是学习一个线性模型或决策树（本质上是一种分段线性模型），只要我们合理运用特征映射，就能处理复杂的关系。

  - [18:05:22 - 18:07:00] **Introduction to Unsupervised Learning (Clustering)**

    Now, in an unsupervised learning task, an unlabeled dataset is provided. It looks something like this table: there is no label column, only feature columns. This represents points in a two-dimensional plane. We have Gene 1 and Gene 2, and for each gene, there are values. What we want to do is extract patterns, knowledge, or information from this dataset by grouping similar items together. This is unsupervised learning, also called clustering. In the next two lectures, I will discuss clustering methods as well as dimensionality reduction and visualization methods. Today, we will focus on clustering methods: K-means, K-modes, and Hierarchical clustering.

    现在，在无监督学习任务中，提供的是无标签的数据集。它看起来像这张表：没有标签列，只有特征列。这代表二维平面上的点。我们有基因 1 和基因 2，每个基因都有数值。我们想要做的是通过将相似的项目分组，从这个数据集中提取模式、知识或信息。这就是无监督学习，也称为聚类。在接下来的两节课中，我将讨论聚类方法以及降维和可视化方法。今天，我们将重点讨论聚类方法：K-均值（K-means）、K-众数（K-modes）和层次聚类（Hierarchical clustering）。

  - [18:07:01 - 18:09:24] **The Clustering Problem and Biological Examples**

    Let's look closely at the clustering problem. As I mentioned, it is an unsupervised learning task where unlabeled data are provided. The objective is to discover knowledge about the dataset by grouping similar samples into a cluster. For example, consider a very complex dataset in biology. There are genes (rows) and experiments (columns). In each experiment, the gene expression value is measured—it's just a number. A red dot might mean high expression, while a gray dot means no expression. By clustering, we group similar genes together or group similar experiments together. This gives us experiment clusters, representing experiments with the same expression pattern. We can also cluster on the rows to get genes with similar expression. This helps us identify interesting gene clusters or, if the experiments are on cancer samples, interesting cancer subtypes.

    让我们仔细看看聚类问题。如前所述，这是一个无监督学习任务，提供的是无标签数据。其目标是通过将相似样本分组到聚类中来发现关于数据集的知识。例如，考虑生物学中一个非常复杂的数据集。有基因（行）和实验（列）。在每个实验中，基因表达值被测量——这只是一个数字。红点可能意味着高表达，而灰点意味着无表达。通过聚类，我们将相似的基因分组，或者将相似的实验分组。这样我们就得到了实验聚类，代表具有相同表达模式的实验。我们也可以对行进行聚类，以获得具有相似表达的基因。这有助于我们识别有趣的基因簇，或者如果实验是关于癌症样本的，可以识别有趣的癌症亚型。

  - [18:09:25 - 18:11:18] **Clustering Objective and Visual Intuition**

    Suppose we have a training dataset with `n` samples. Basically, we want to assign each point, each sample, to one of the `K` clusters according to some optimization criteria. Here, the criterion is to maximize the within-cluster similarity under a similarity metric. Consider these data points. We might cluster them in one way, giving us a solution for `K=2`. But this result might not be good; you can see the points in the bottom cluster are far from each other. We can also cluster them in a different way, which looks better. If we increase the number of clusters from two to three, we might get a result that looks even better than the previous ones. So, the problem is fundamentally about looking for the best grouping.

    假设我们有一个包含 `n` 个样本的训练数据集。基本上，我们要根据某种优化标准将每个点、每个样本分配到 `K` 个聚类中的一个。在这里，标准是在某种相似性度量下最大化簇内相似度。看看这些数据点。我们可以用一种方式对它们进行聚类，得到 `K=2` 的解。但这可能不是好的结果；你可以看到底部聚类中的点彼此距离很远。我们要可以用另一种方式聚类，这看起来更好。如果我们把聚类数量从两个增加到三个，我们可能会得到一个比之前看起来更好的结果。所以，这个问题的根本在于寻找最佳的分组方式。

  - [18:11:19 - 18:14:23] **Similarity Metrics: Euclidean vs. Manhattan Distance**

    To do this, we need a metric. We need to define which data points are similar and which are not. An ideal metric should satisfy these conditions: small distance means more similar; large distance means more dissimilar. Two popular distances are the Euclidean distance and the Manhattan distance. Let `k` be the number of features (not the number of clusters). For two points in a 1-dimensional space (on a line), the Euclidean and Manhattan distances are equal; they are just the absolute value of the difference. However, in a 2-dimensional feature space, they are defined differently. The Euclidean distance is the square root of the sum of squared differences in each dimension: `E(A,B) = √((a_1-b_1)^2 + (a_2-b_2)^2)`. The Manhattan distance is the sum of the absolute values of the differences: `M(A,B) = |a_1-b_1| + |a_2-b_2|`. In a high-dimensional feature space, these two distances differ. The Manhattan distance is typically slightly larger than the Euclidean distance.

    为了做到这一点，我们需要一个度量标准。我们需要定义哪些数据点是相似的，哪些是不相似的。理想的度量应满足这些条件：距离小意味着更相似，距离大意味着更不相似。两种流行的距离是欧几里得距离（Euclidean distance）和曼哈顿距离（Manhattan distance）。设 `k` 为特征的数量（注意不是聚类的数量）。对于一维空间（直线上）的两个点，欧几里得距离和曼哈顿距离是相等的，都是差值的绝对值。然而，在二维特征空间中，它们的定义是不同的。欧几里得距离是各维度差值平方和的平方根：`E(A,B) = √((a_1-b_1)^2 + (a_2-b_2)^2)`。曼哈顿距离是各维度差值绝对值的和：`M(A,B) = |a_1-b_1| + |a_2-b_2|`。在高维特征空间中，这两个距离是不同的。曼哈顿距离通常比欧几里得距离稍大。

  - [18:14:24 - 18:15:02] **Geometric Interpretation of Distances**

    If you look at the difference here visually, putting them in the same picture: the Euclidean distance corresponds to the diagonal edge (the hypotenuse), while the Manhattan distance follows the "streets," like going from one shop to another along a city block grid.

    如果你在同一张图中直观地对比这种差异：欧几里得距离对应于对角边（斜边），而曼哈顿距离则像是沿着城市街区网格“走街道”，就像从一家商店走到另一家商店一样。

  - [18:15:03 - 18:17:59] **Pearson Correlation for Time Series**

    We also have other distances for different types of datasets. For time series data points, we use the Pearson correlation coefficient as the metric. This coefficient is equal to the covariance of the two points (vectors) divided by the product of their standard deviations. The Pearson correlation coefficient ranges between -1 and 1. This metric measures linear association only. If the coefficient is 1, the two points have a perfect positive linear relationship. For example, if you have vectors `S` and `T` located on a line passing through the origin, the value is 1. If one point is here and another is there such that they have a perfect negative relationship, the correlation is -1. A value of 0 means no linear relationship. For instance, if vector `S` and vector `T` form a 90-degree angle relative to the origin, the Pearson correlation is 0. This is used mainly for time series data.

    针对不同类型的数据集，我们还有其他的距离度量。对于时间序列数据点，我们使用皮尔逊相关系数（Pearson correlation coefficient）作为度量。该系数等于两点（向量）的协方差除以它们标准差的乘积。皮尔逊相关系数的范围在 -1 到 1 之间。这个指标仅衡量线性相关性。如果系数为 1，则两点具有完美的正线性关系。例如，如果向量 `S` 和 `T` 位于通过原点的同一条直线上，该值为 1。如果它们呈完美的负相关关系，相关系数为 -1。值为 0 意味着没有线性关系。例如，如果向量 `S` 和向量 `T` 相对于原点形成 90 度角，则皮尔逊相关系数为 0。这主要用于时间序列数据。

  - [18:18:00 - 18:21:20] **Hamming Distance for Categorical Data**

    We also have the Hamming distance. Hamming distance is defined for strings of the same length. It equals the number of positions in which the two strings have different letters. For example, if we have the string `ACTGA` and the string `ATTGG`, we align them. You will see different letters in the second position (`C` vs `T`) and the last position (`A` vs `G`). In other positions, they have the same letter. Therefore, the Hamming distance is 2. In computer science, we often talk about 0-1 strings. If we compare `00110` and `01011`, the positions differ at index 1, 2, and 4. So, this is a Hamming distance of 3. Most importantly, we can use this to measure data points with non-numeric, categorical features. For example, consider a person's record: `(Red, Small, Male, Urban)`. Another person's record is `(Blue, Small, Female, Urban)`. The Hamming distance between these two records is 2 because the color is different (`Red` vs `Blue`) and the gender is different (`Male` vs `Female`). So, we use this distance when clustering samples with categorical features.

    我们还有汉明距离（Hamming distance）。汉明距离定义用于相同长度的字符串。它等于两个字符串中字符不同的位置数量。例如，如果我们有字符串 `ACTGA` 和字符串 `ATTGG`，我们将它们对齐。你会看到在第二个位置（`C` 对 `T`）和最后一个位置（`A` 对 `G`）字符不同。在其他位置，字符是相同的。因此，汉明距离是 2。在计算机科学中，我们经常讨论 0-1 字符串。如果我们比较 `00110` 和 `01011`，它们在第 2、3 和 5 位不同（索引 1, 2, 4）。所以，汉明距离是 3。最重要的是，我们可以用它来度量具有非数值分类特征的数据点。例如，考虑一个人的记录：`(红, 小, 男, 城市)`。另一个人的记录是 `(蓝, 小, 女, 城市)`。这两条记录之间的汉明距离是 2，因为颜色不同（`红` 对 `蓝`）且性别不同（`男` 对 `女`）。因此，我们在对具有分类特征的样本进行聚类时使用这种距离。

  - [18:21:21 - 18:25:03] **Applications of Clustering**

    Clustering has many applications and is widely used in data science. For example, we can apply clustering methods to classify customers to provide precise recommendations. Some customers may want to eat seafood, so we assign that information to them. In the financial market, we can classify stocks or other financial products to prepare investment portfolios, identifying which are suitable for long-term versus short-term investment to diversify your money. You can also use clustering to identify outliers in a dataset. For instance, using bank transaction records, you could potentially identify terrorists because they transfer large amounts of money frequently from everywhere to everywhere. This is anomaly detection. Of course, you can also use social network data to identify groups of people with the same political opinions during voting times. In science, for example with genetic data, we can divide cancers into different subtypes for better treatment. We also use it to classify bacteria into different species. This is not obvious because we usually cannot see bacteria or know their size and shape; we can only base the classification on DNA or other genetic information.

    聚类有许多应用，在数据科学中被广泛使用。例如，我们可以应用聚类方法对客户进行分类，以提供精准的推荐。有些客户可能想吃海鲜，我们就把相关信息推给他们。在金融市场，我们可以对股票或其他金融产品进行分类，以准备投资组合，识别哪些适合长期投资，哪些适合短期投资，从而分散资金风险。你也可以利用聚类来识别数据集中的异常值。例如，利用银行交易记录，你可能识别出恐怖分子，因为他们经常从各地进行大额转账。这就是异常检测。当然，你也可以利用社交网络数据在投票期间识别具有相同政治观点的群体。在科学领域，例如利用基因数据，我们可以将癌症分为不同的亚型以进行更好的治疗。我们也用它将细菌分类为不同的物种。这并不显而易见，因为我们通常看不到细菌，也不知道它们的大小和形状；我们只能基于 DNA 或其他遗传信息进行分类。

  - [18:25:04 - 18:26:24] **K-Means Algorithm: Concept and Centroids**

    Now, we move to the first method: the K-means method. The idea is very simple. We specify the number of clusters first. We just assign the data points into this many non-overlapping clusters iteratively. Looking at this data, three clusters seem reasonable. In the K-means method, each cluster is represented by a centroid, which is the arithmetic mean of the points in the cluster. For example, if you have several points, the arithmetic mean is just the sum of the points divided by the number of points. Of course, each point has values for multiple features. When I say "sum," I mean we sum the values feature-wise. We separate the features and do the sum for each. This is the mathematical expression: `P = (1/t) * (P_1 + P_2 + ... + P_t)`.

    现在，我们要讲第一种方法：K-均值（K-means）方法。它的主要思想非常简单。我们首先指定聚类的数量。然后我们要迭代地将数据点分配到这些互不重叠的聚类中。看这些数据，分成三个聚类似乎是合理的。在 K-means 方法中，每个聚类由一个质心（centroid）表示，它是该聚类中所有点的算术平均值。例如，如果你有几个点，算术平均值就是所有点的和除以点的数量。当然，每个点都有多个特征值。当我们说“求和”时，是指按特征分别求和。我们把特征分开，对每一个特征进行求和。数学表达式是：`P = (1/t) * (P_1 + P_2 + ... + P_t)`。

  - [18:26:25 - 18:31:36] **Minimizing Within-Cluster Variation (WCV)**

    K-means tries to obtain the best result by minimizing the Within-Cluster Variation (WCV). Suppose we divide the data points into `K` clusters. For each cluster, we calculate a number called the within-cluster variation. If we use Euclidean distance, this is defined as the sum of the squared Euclidean distance from each point to the center, divided by the number of points in the cluster—basically taking the average. For example, if we have a four-point cluster, the WCV is the average of the squared lengths of the segments connecting the points to the centroid. We calculate this for all `K` clusters and sum them together. We take the average because we don't want to penalize large clusters. K-means partitions the data points to minimize this total WCV. Why use this objective function? Because a small WCV implies the points are tightly grouped. If we have a large WCV, the points are widely spread. Looking at two examples, the one with tightly grouped points definitely looks better.

    K-means 试图通过最小化簇内变异（Within-Cluster Variation, WCV）来获得最佳结果。假设我们将数据点分为 `K` 个聚类。对于每个聚类，我们计算一个称为簇内变异的数值。如果我们使用欧几里得距离，这被定义为每个点到中心的欧几里得距离的平方和，除以聚类中的点数——基本上就是取平均值。例如，如果我们有一个包含四个点的聚类，WCV 就是连接点到质心的线段长度平方的平均值。我们对所有 `K` 个聚类计算这个值并将它们相加。我们取平均值是因为我们不想惩罚大的聚类。K-means 对数据点进行划分以最小化这个总 WCV。为什么要使用这个目标函数？因为较小的 WCV 意味着点在聚类中紧密地聚集在一起。如果我们有一个很大的 WCV，说明点分布得很散。看这两个例子，点聚集得很紧密的那个看起来肯定更好。

  - [18:31:37 - 18:36:23] **The K-Means Algorithm Steps**

    In summary, the K-means algorithm works like this:

    1. Specify the number `K` of clusters. This is a hyperparameter the analyst has to set.

    2. Randomly initialize `K` centroids.

    3. Repeatedly do the following:

       - **Assignment:** Assign each point to its closest centroid. For example, if `x_1` is closer to the red centroid than the blue one, it is assigned to the red cluster. However, for a point like `x_7`, if we assigned it to the red cluster, it would violate the proximity condition because it is closer to the blue centroid. So, we must assign `x_7` to the blue cluster. Assigning points to the closest centroid ensures a tighter cluster and smaller WCV.

       - **Update:** Compute the new centroid of each cluster. We calculate this by summing the points and dividing by the number of points in the cluster.

         We repeat these two steps until the centroid positions do not change, meaning we have a stable cluster result.

    总之，K-means 算法是这样工作的：

    1. 指定聚类数量 `K`。这是分析师必须设置的超参数。

    2. 随机初始化 `K` 个质心。

    3. 重复执行以下操作：

       - **分配（Assignment）：** 将每个点分配给离它最近的质心。例如，如果 `x_1` 离红色质心比离蓝色质心更近，它就被分配到红色聚类。然而，对于像 `x_7` 这样的点，如果我们把它分配给红色聚类，就会违反邻近条件，因为它离蓝色质心更近。所以，我们必须把 `x_7` 分配给蓝色聚类。将点分配给最近的质心可以确保聚类更紧密，WCV 更小。

       - **更新（Update）：** 计算每个聚类的新质心。我们通过将点相加并除以聚类中的点数来计算。

         我们重复这两个步骤，直到质心位置不再改变，这意味着我们得到了稳定的聚类结果。

  - [18:36:24 - 18:41:35] **1D K-Means Example**

    Let's look at a 1-dimensional example to see how we do this step-by-step. Consider 4 points at coordinates 0, 2, 10, and 12. Let's assign `K=2`.

    **Initialization:** We assign two centroids. Let's pick the first centroid at 0 (the leftmost point) and the second centroid at 2 (the second leftmost point).

    **Step 1 (Assignment):** The point at 0 is definitely in Cluster 1 (distance 0). The point at 2 is definitely in Cluster 2 (distance 0). The point at 10 is distance 8 from Cluster 2 (at 2) and distance 10 from Cluster 1 (at 0), so it belongs to Cluster 2. Similarly, the point at 12 belongs to Cluster 2.

    **Step 1 (Update):** Cluster 1 has only one point (0), so the new centroid is 0. Cluster 2 has three points (2, 10, 12). The average is `(2 + 10 + 12) / 3 = 24 / 3 = 8`. So the new centroid for Cluster 2 is at coordinate 8.

    **Step 2 (Assignment):** Now we reassign based on new centroids (0 and 8). Point 0 is close to 0 -> Cluster 1. Point 2 is distance 2 from Cluster 1 (at 0) and distance 6 from Cluster 2 (at 8). Since 2 < 6, Point 2 moves to Cluster 1. Points 10 and 12 are closer to 8, so they stay in Cluster 2.

    **Step 2 (Update):** Cluster 1 now has points (0, 2). The average is `(0+2)/2 = 1`. Cluster 2 has points (10, 12). The average is `(10+12)/2 = 11`. The new centroids are 1 and 11.

    If we run another round, the result will be stable. The membership hasn't changed, so the centroids won't change. This is the whole process.

    让我们看一个一维的例子，逐步了解它是如何运作的。考虑坐标为 0、2、10 和 12 的 4 个点。设 `K=2`。

    **初始化：** 我们分配两个质心。假设我们选第一个质心在 0（最左边的点），第二个质心在 2（左边第二个点）。

    **步骤 1（分配）：** 点 0 肯定在聚类 1 中（距离 0）。点 2 肯定在聚类 2 中（距离 0）。点 10 距离聚类 2（位置 2）的距离是 8，距离聚类 1（位置 0）的距离是 10，所以它属于聚类 2。同样，点 12 也属于聚类 2。

    **步骤 1（更新）：** 聚类 1 只有一个点（0），所以新质心是 0。聚类 2 有三个点（2, 10, 12）。平均值是 `(2 + 10 + 12) / 3 = 24 / 3 = 8`。所以聚类 2 的新质心在坐标 8。

    **步骤 2（分配）：** 现在我们根据新质心（0 和 8）重新分配。点 0 离 0 近 -> 聚类 1。点 2 距离聚类 1（位置 0）为 2，距离聚类 2（位置 8）为 6。因为 2 < 6，点 2 移动到聚类 1。点 10 和 12 离 8 更近，所以它们留在聚类 2。

    **步骤 2（更新）：** 聚类 1 现在有点（0, 2）。平均值是 `(0+2)/2 = 1`。聚类 2 有点（10, 12）。平均值是 `(10+12)/2 = 11`。新质心是 1 和 11。

    如果我们再跑一轮，结果是稳定的。成员资格没有改变，所以质心也不会改变。这就是整个过程。

  - [18:41:36 - 18:43:46] **2D K-Means Visualization**

    In one dimension, it is trivial. In two dimensions with more clusters, it is not trivial. For example, if we place centroids initially, we get an initial clustering. The purple cluster might take one point, the red one only two points. When we recalculate the centroid, the centroid might move significantly. We update the clusters based on the new centroids. We do this iteratively, adjusting the membership of each cluster slightly in every step until we have stable clusters. Sometimes it takes many rounds, sometimes just a couple.

    在一维情况下，这很简单。但在聚类较多的二维情况下，这就不是那么简单了。例如，如果我们初始化质心，我们会得到一个初始聚类。紫色聚类可能包含一个点，红色聚类可能只有两个点。当我们重新计算质心时，质心可能会发生显著移动。我们根据新的质心更新聚类。我们迭代地做这件事，每一步稍微调整每个聚类的成员，直到我们得到稳定的聚类。有时这需要很多轮，有时只需要几轮。

  - [18:43:47 - 18:48:13] **Pros, Cons, and Issue 1 (Initialization)**

    Is the K-means algorithm clear? Okay. Here are the strengths and weaknesses. The first pro is that it is very simple. Because it is simple, it is fast and works well on very large datasets. Therefore, K-means is widely used in data science and machine learning. However, there are a series of issues.

    **Issue 1:** The final result depends on the initial location of the centroids. Using different initial centroids on the same dataset can produce different clusters with similar quality.

    **Solutions:**

    1. Run the algorithm a number of times and take the best result (the one with the minimal WCV).
    2. Use a smart initialization method, such as **K-means++** (available in Python). The idea of K-means++ is simple: choose the first centroid randomly. Then, choose the second centroid as far as possible from the first one. For the third one, consider the positions of the existing two and find a point far from them. This is the default implementation in Python's `sklearn`.

    K-means 算法清楚了吗？好的。这是它的优缺点。第一个优点是它非常简单。正因为它简单，所以速度快，并且在非常大的数据集上表现良好。因此，K-means 在数据科学和机器学习中被广泛使用。然而，它也有一系列问题。

    **问题 1：** 最终结果取决于质心的初始位置。在同一数据集上使用不同的初始质心可能会产生质量相似但不同的聚类结果。

    **解决方案：**

    1. 运行算法多次，并取最好的结果（WCV 最小的那个）。
    2. 使用智能初始化方法，例如 **K-means++**（Python 中可用）。K-means++ 的思路很简单：随机选择第一个质心。然后，选择离第一个质心尽可能远的第二个质心。对于第三个质心，考虑现有两个质心的位置，并找到一个离它们都很远的点。这是 Python `sklearn` 中的默认实现。

  - [18:48:14 - 18:54:20] **Issue 2 (Choosing K) and The Elbow Method**

    **Issue 2:** How do we choose `K`? The hyperparameter `K` must be decided before we run the algorithm. If a dataset contains millions of high-dimensional points, we cannot visualize them to guess `K`.

    **Solution 1: Prior Knowledge.** For some applications, you have prior knowledge. For example, partitioning countries into three groups (underdeveloped, developing, developed) based on GDP and population suggests `K=3`. Sometimes, you can verify if a result is useful. If you classify breast cancer into two types but the survival rates for the clusters are not significantly different, the result is not useful for doctors. This suggests a two-cluster solution is too rough, and you should try 5 or 6 types.

    **Solution 2: The Elbow Method.** We search for a good `K` by trying different values (2, 3, 4, 5...) and plotting the **Total Within-Cluster Variation** against the number of clusters. With 1 cluster, the variance is large. With 2 clusters, it decreases significantly. With 3, it decreases again. The more clusters you have, the better the solution (lower variance). However, there is a **turning point** (elbow). Before this point (e.g., going from 1 to 3), quality improves significantly. After this point, improvement is slight. We choose this turning point (e.g., `K=3`).

    **问题 2：** 我们如何选择 `K`？超参数 `K` 必须在运行算法之前确定。如果一个数据集包含数百万个高维点，我们无法通过可视化来猜测 `K`。

    **解决方案 1：先验知识。** 对于某些应用，你有先验知识。例如，根据 GDP 和人口将国家分为三组（不发达、发展中、发达），这表明 `K=3`。有时，你可以验证结果是否有用。如果你将乳腺癌分为两类，但这两个聚类的存活率没有显著差异，那么这个结果对医生来说就没有用。这表明两个聚类的方案太粗糙了，你应该尝试 5 或 6 种类型。

    **解决方案 2：肘部法则（Elbow Method）。** 我们通过尝试不同的值（2, 3, 4, 5...）并绘制 **总簇内变异（Total Within-Cluster Variation）** 与聚类数量的关系图来寻找好的 `K`。如果只有 1 个聚类，变异很大。有 2 个聚类时，变异显著下降。有 3 个时，再次下降。聚类越多，解越好（变异越低）。然而，这里有一个 **转折点**（肘部）。在这个点之前（例如从 1 到 3），质量显著提高。在这个点之后，提高很微小。我们选择这个转折点（例如 `K=3`）。

  - [18:54:21 - 18:58:42] **The Silhouette Method**

    **Solution 3: The Silhouette Method.** This considers two measures:

    1. **Cohesion (`c(i)`):** The average distance from a point to the centroid in its own cluster. A smaller cohesion implies tighter clustering.

    2. **Separation (`s(i)`):** The average distance from a point to the points in the *nearest* other cluster. We want the distance between points from different clusters to be large.

       We define the Silhouette score `r(i)` as: `r(i) = (s(i) - c(i)) / max(c(i), s(i))`. This value is between -1 and 1. A larger `r(i)` means better clustering. If we run K-means for different `K`, we get different average Silhouette scores. Unlike the Elbow method (which always decreases), the Silhouette score will go up and then down. We choose the `K` with the highest score (e.g., `K=6` in the example).

    **解决方案 3：轮廓系数法（Silhouette Method）。** 这考虑了两个指标：

    1. **内聚度（Cohesion, `c(i)`）：** 点到其自身聚类质心的平均距离。较小的内聚度意味着聚类更紧密。

    2. **分离度（Separation, `s(i)`）：** 点到*最近*的其他聚类中所有点的平均距离。我们希望不同聚类的点之间的距离尽可能大。

       我们定义轮廓系数 `r(i)` 为：`r(i) = (s(i) - c(i)) / max(c(i), s(i))`。该值在 -1 到 1 之间。较大的 `r(i)` 意味着更好的聚类。如果我们针对不同的 `K` 运行 K-means，我们会得到不同的平均轮廓分数。与肘部法则（总是下降）不同，轮廓分数会先上升后下降。我们选择分数最高的 `K`（例如示例中的 `K=6`）。

  - [18:58:43 - 19:02:28] **Website Demo and Break**

    There is a nice commercial website (`numiqo.com`) that demonstrates this. They run the Elbow method to automatically choose `K`. For K-means, we can only use numerical features like salary, age, and weight. In their example, they chose three clusters. The visualization shows how the data points are assigned. The dataset isn't perfect, but it shows the ideas. Okay, I think that's the first half of today's lecture. Let's have a ten-minute break.

    有一个很好的商业网站（`numiqo.com`）展示了这一点。他们运行肘部法则来自动选择 `K`。对于 K-means，我们只能使用像薪水、年龄和体重这样的数值特征。在他们的例子中，他们选择了三个聚类。可视化展示了数据点是如何分配的。这个数据集并不完美，但它展示了这个思路。好的，我想这就是今天课程的前半部分。我们休息十分钟。
