    DBSCAN 是另一种强大的聚类工具，因为它基于密度识别聚类，并且可以发现任意形状的簇，而不像 K-means 那样假设簇是球形的。你必须掌握两个关键参数：Epsilon（半径）和 MinPts（最小点数）。准备好根据这些定义识别核心点、边界点和噪声/离散点。DBSCAN 的算法步骤——选取未访问点并扩展密集区域——非常适合作为考试题。

  - [20:30:58 - 20:33:39] **Neural Networks: Structure and Parameters**

    Neural networks are perhaps the most important part of our review. I expect you to understand the architecture: the input layer, hidden layers, and the output layer. You must be familiar with various activation functions like ReLU, Sigmoid, Tanh, and Softmax, including their advantages and limitations.

    A practical skill I will test is the ability to calculate the number of parameters in a network. The rule is simple: every link between neurons represents a weight (a parameter), and every neuron typically has a bias. By summing these up across layers, you get the total parameter count. While the full backpropagation training process is complicated with many notations, you should understand the basic idea of forward propagation to compute output and backpropagation to compute gradients for weight updates.

    神经网络可能是我们复习中最重要的部分。我希望你们理解其架构：输入层、隐藏层和输出层。你们必须熟悉各种激活函数，如 ReLU、Sigmoid、Tanh 和 Softmax，包括它们的优缺点。

    我会考察的一项实际技能是计算网络中参数数量的能力。规则很简单：神经元之间的每个连接代表一个权重（参数），而每个神经元通常有一个偏置（Bias）。通过逐层累加这些参数，你就能得到总参数量。虽然完整的反向传播训练过程涉及很多符号，比较复杂，但你应该理解基本思想：通过前向传播计算输出，通过反向传播计算梯度，从而更新权重。

  - [20:33:39 - 20:35:44] **Deep Learning Challenges and Architectures**

    In deep learning, we discussed the "Double Descent" hypothesis. This is the idea that even if you have more than enough parameters, you can actually achieve better results; the model finds a simpler representation that generalizes well. This is a very important conceptual takeaway.

    When designing a proper neural network, you must solve the vanishing and exploding gradient problems. Vanishing gradients mean the updates become too small for the model to learn, while exploding gradients mean they become too large, preventing convergence. This is why architectures like CNNs and RNNs were developed—to handle specific data types and training issues more effectively.

    在深度学习中，我们讨论了“双下降”（Double Descent）假设。这个观点认为，即使参数量远超需求，实际上也可能获得更好的结果；模型会找到一种泛化能力很强的简单表示。这是一个非常重要的概念性结论。

    在设计合理的神经网络时，必须解决梯度消失和梯度爆炸问题。梯度消失意味着更新变得太小，模型无法学习；而梯度爆炸意味着更新过大，导致模型无法收敛。这就是为什么我们要开发 CNN 和 RNN 等架构——为了更有效地处理特定的数据类型和训练问题。

  - [20:35:44 - 20:38:45] **CNNs and RNNs**

    For Convolutional Neural Networks (CNNs), you need to understand the structure: filters, kernels, and channels. You should be able to calculate how many parameters or channels are in a layer given the filter size and number of filters. Remember the key properties: local connectivity, parameter sharing, and translation invariance. CNNs build a hierarchy, starting from edges in early layers to full objects in deeper layers.

    For Recurrent Neural Networks (RNNs), the focus is on sequential data and temporal dependencies. You must understand the concept of the hidden state (h_t), which acts as the "memory" of previous inputs. Mathematically, you can think of it as a generalization of a Hidden Markov Model. RNNs are ideal for time-series forecasting and NLP, though they struggle with long-term dependencies due to those same gradient issues we mentioned. You should be able to visualize or draw the connection between different time steps and layers.

    对于卷积神经网络（CNN），你需要理解其结构：滤波器（Filters）、卷积核（Kernels）和通道（Channels）。给定滤波器的大小和数量，你应该能计算出一层中有多少个参数或通道。记住其关键特性：局部连接、参数共享和平移不变性。CNN 构建了一个层次结构，从早期层提取边缘，到深层提取完整物体。

    对于循环神经网络（RNN），重点在于序列数据和时间依赖性。你必须理解隐藏状态（h_t）的概念，它充当了先前输入的“记忆”。从数学上讲，你可以将其视为隐马尔可夫模型的推广。RNN 非常适合时间序列预测和自然语言处理（NLP），尽管由于我们提到的梯度问题，它们在处理长期依赖方面存在困难。你应该能够可视化或画出不同时间步和层之间的连接关系。

  - [20:38:45 - 20:44:14] **Exam Logistics and Q&A**

    To answer your questions about the exam format: since this is a graduate-level course, the exam will be 2.5 hours long. I need to include enough calculation questions to justify that time. There will be about three to five main questions, each with several sub-questions.

    Don't worry about complex log calculations. I honestly forgot how to use the log function on a standard calculator myself, so I won't expect you to do it either! The numerical questions will be manageable—for example, calculating Euclidean distance in two dimensions is very simple and doesn't require a specialized calculator. Every problem, even calculation-based ones, can technically be converted into a multiple-choice format (MCQ) if needed, but the point is that you still need to perform the calculation to find the correct answer among the distractors.

    回答你们关于考试形式的问题：因为这是一门研究生课程，考试时长为 2.5 小时。为了匹配这个时长，我需要加入足够的计算题。大概会有三到五个大题，每个大题包含几个小题。

    不用担心复杂的对数计算。老实说，我自己都忘了怎么在标准计算器上用对数函数了，所以我也不指望你们会用！数值题会比较容易处理——例如，计算二维空间的欧氏距离非常简单，不需要专门的计算器。每个问题，甚至是计算题，技术上都可以根据需要转换为多选题（MCQ），但重点是，你仍然需要通过计算在干扰项中找到正确答案。

  - [20:44:14 - 20:51:31] **Final Project and Closing Remarks**

    放轻松，你们中的大多数人已经通过平时考核拿到了大约 30 分。只要复习好我们今天讨论的核心概念，就不会有问题。回头见。

  ```py
  import pandas as pd
  data = pd.read_csv("Mall_Customer.csv")
  X = data[['Annual Income (k$)', 'Spending SCore (1-100)']]
  ```
- For clustering, students may use Annual Income and Spending Score

  - Logical organization and clarity
***
Linkage Methods

We know how to calculate the distance between points (Euclidean, Manhattan), but how do we calculate the distance between clusters? This is called "Linkage," and there are four main ways to define it:

Single Linkage: The minimum distance between any point in one cluster and any point in the other. It uses the closest pair of points.

Complete Linkage: The maximum distance. It uses the furthest pair of points between the two clusters.

Average Linkage: The mean distance. You calculate all possible pairwise distances between the points in Cluster A and Cluster B, sum them up, and divide by the total number of pairs. For a 3-point cluster and a 2-point cluster, you compute 6 distances and average them.

Centroid Linkage: The distance between the centroids of the two clusters.
Different linkage methods produce different results. In the example I showed, different linkages revealed different gene clusters. It's hard to say which is "best"; it depends on your application. In biology, one method might reveal an informative subtype while another reveals a different but equally valid pattern.
***

Here are the finalized main changes made to your project, summarized for your report:

- **Silhouette Analysis**: Added mathematical validation comparing $K$ values (2 through 6) to prove that **$K=5$** offers the best balance between cluster cohesion and business interpretability.
- **DBSCAN Optimization**: Implemented a **k-Distance Plot** to scientifically determine the `epsilon` value ($eps=1.0$), reducing noise and revealing significant anomalies.
- **Hierarchical Clustering**: Integrated a **Dendrogram** using **Ward Linkage** (Lecture 5) to minimize within-cluster variance and show the "family tree" of customer segments.
- **PCA (Principal Component Analysis)**: Visualized the global data structure in 2D, capturing **78% of the total variance** to confirm that the clusters are mathematically distinct.
- **t-SNE & UMAP**: Deployed these state-of-the-art non-linear manifold techniques to prove that clusters remain tightly grouped and separated even in complex local neighborhoods.
- **3D Feature Space**: Developed a **3D Scatter Plot** of Age, Income, and Spending Score using a custom "Corporate Teal" colormap to visualize the "Golden Clusters" in their natural high-dimensional state.
- **Outlier Profiling**: Specifically analyzed the 2 DBSCAN outliers as **"Niche High-Net-Worth"** individuals, providing a tailored strategy for elite, high-income customers who defy standard spending patterns.
- **Strategic Business Insights**: Linked technical findings to retail strategies, such as creating **loyalty programs** to address the "Spending Cliff" observed at age 40+.
